# Normative Rule Traceability — Ade

> **Status:** Living architectural document. Regenerated by `/traceability`; not hand-edited.
>
> **HEAD:** `a3a0636` · **Generated:** 2026-05-30 · **Baseline:** `67d1ccc` (`.idd-config.json` `head_deltas_baseline`)

This document is the **invariant ↔ enforcement audit** IDD §10 demands. For every rule the project commits to, it traces *where the rule is specified* → *where it is enforced in code* → *which tests prove it* → *which CI check fails the build on violation*. A rule that cannot fill all four cells is an **enforcement gap**; this doc surfaces gaps rather than hiding them.

## Source of rules

The canonical source is the **invariant registry** at `docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml` (`.idd-config.json` `invariant_registry`). This doc is a join: registry entries × codebase introspection. Rule IDs, families, names, sources, and the registry-recorded `tests` / `ci_script` / `ci_scripts` / `code_locus` fields come from the registry; each test name and CI script is cross-checked for existence on disk at HEAD `a3a0636`, and divergences are flagged inline as **drift**. (Verification this pass is grep/ls only — no build or test execution.)

Normative documents (per `.idd-config.json` `normative_docs`): `docs/active/CE-79_gate_statement.md`, `docs/active/CE-79_tier5_addendum.md`, `docs/active/comparison_surface_contract.md`, `docs/active/shelley_bootstrap_contract.md`, `docs/active/CE-73_reclassification.md`, `CLAUDE.md`. The registry `source` field resolves into these plus the per-cluster planning docs under `docs/planning/` and cluster docs under `docs/clusters/` (closed clusters under `docs/clusters/completed/`).

## Conventions

- **Families** are the registry ID-prefix scheme: `T` (true), `DC` (derived), `CN` (constraint-network / classification table), `RO` (release obligation), `OP` (operational). The registry `tier` field (true / derived / operational / release / constraint) is noted per rule; it does not always coincide with the ID prefix (e.g. some `CN-*` and `DC-*` entries carry `tier = "release"`).
- **Status** is the registry `status`: `enforced` (Code+Tests+CI present and load-bearing), `partial` (some cells filled, scope-limited), `declared` (named but not yet mechanically enforced — an open enforcement gap by design).
- A **Code / Tests / CI** cell reading `_(no … — gap)_` is an explicit enforcement gap, not an omission.
- **[not found on disk — drift]** (tests) / **[not on disk — drift]** (CI) flags a registry-named test/CI that could not be located in the working tree at HEAD `a3a0636` — a registry↔code coherence gap to reconcile (rename the registry entry or restore the artifact). Test drift is resolved against the **leaf** function name (the segment after the last `::`).

### `DC-CINPUT-01`: Warm-start verification CAPABILITY for the recovered seed-epoch consensus inputs (authority surface — NOT production restart)

_tier: derived · status: partial · introduced: PHASE4-N-F-A_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-A/cluster.md; A3a-wal-provenance-entry.md; A3b-warm-start-restore.md |
| **Requirement** | The seed-epoch consensus-input import is a replay-reconstructable WAL fact (additive closed `WalEntry::SeedEpochConsensusInputsImported`, distinct tag, NOT in the AdmitBlock prior_fp/post_fp chain; WAL append is the commit point). Replay reconstructs exactly one typed `RecoveredBootstrapProvenance` per store/anchor (duplicate or anchor-mismatch fails closed); `bootstrap_initial_state`'s warm-start branch (`RequiredFromRecoveredProvenance`) restores the sidecar and verifies it fail-closed (present, `blake2b_256 == provenance.sidecar_hash`, A1 decode, anchor_fp + epoch_no binding, byte-identity re-encode) or halts (typed `BootstrapError`, `EXIT_AUTHORITY_FATAL_DECODE`, no bundle fallback). **Proven on the AUTHORITY SURFACE only** (`bootstrap_initial_state` exercised directly); **no production mode is wired to it** (`node.rs` `run_node_until_shutdown` + `recover_node_state` are test-only; `produce_mode` cold-starts). |
| **Code** | crates/ade_ledger/src/wal/event.rs (`SeedEpochConsensusInputsImported`, tag 3); crates/ade_ledger/src/wal/replay.rs (`ReplayOutcome` + `RecoveredBootstrapProvenance`); crates/ade_runtime/src/seed_consensus_provenance.rs (append helper); crates/ade_runtime/src/bootstrap.rs (`SeedEpochConsensusSource`, `BootstrapState`, `restore_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs`) |
| **Tests** | `wal_seed_cinput_entry_round_trips_byte_identical`, `replay_yields_bootstrap_provenance_view`, `replay_rejects_duplicate_provenance_entry`, `replay_rejects_anchor_mismatched_provenance_entry`, `admit_block_chain_unaffected_by_provenance_entry`, `warm_start_restores_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs_byte_identical`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_missing_sidecar`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_hash_mismatch`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_anchor_mismatch`, `warm_start_fails_closed_on_epoch_mismatch`, `warm_start_required_provenance_rejects_malformed_sidecar`, `warm_start_never_falls_back_to_consensus_inputs_path` |
| **CI** | _(no CI script — gap)_ |

> **Open obligation (deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C, NOT a defect).** The warm-start VERIFICATION CAPABILITY is enforced at the authority surface (A3b; the 12 tests above resolve on disk). The **PRODUCTION restart path** — a production mode that opens a persistent store + `FileWalStore`, replays to a `RecoveredBootstrapProvenance`, and calls `bootstrap_initial_state(RequiredFromRecoveredProvenance)` — is NOT wired (`node.rs` `run_node_until_shutdown` + `recover_node_state` are test-only). This is why the rule is `partial`, not `enforced`. Deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C (C3); reopen when a production mode threads the recovery path.

### `DC-CRYPTO-03`: VRF signing transcript equivalence and verification symmetry. For canonical inputs (slot, epoch_nonce, vrf_signing_key, vrf_role) the RED signer produces a VrfProof byte-identical to cardano-node's reference output, and the emitted VrfProof verifies under ade_crypto::vrf::verify_praos_vrf with the matching verification key. Private-key execution is RED-shell confined; BLUE consumes the VrfProof as a captured signed artifact.

### `DC-CRYPTO-04`: KES signing transcript equivalence and verification symmetry. For canonical inputs (kes_secret, period, msg) the RED signer produces a KesSignature byte-identical to Haskell cardano-base's Sum6KES reference and verifying under ade_crypto::kes::verify_kes. After PHASE4-N-P S5 the algorithm is BLUE-owned (ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes); cross-impl agreement with the Haskell reference is mechanically validated against a cardano-cli ground-truth corpus (DC-CRYPTO-08). Private-key execution is RED-shell confined; BLUE consumes the KesSignature as a captured signed artifact.

### `DC-CRYPTO-05`: KES evolution discipline: evolve(k_i) -> k_{i+1} is one-way. The evolved key signs period i+1 and MUST NOT sign for period i. RED kes_sign is forbidden when the requested period > current_period + evolutions_remaining; kes_evolve is forbidden when to < from or to > from + evolutions_remaining. Forward secrecy is a RED-shell discipline; BLUE has no recovery path if RED violates it. After PHASE4-N-P S5 the underlying algorithm (`ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::update_kes`) is BLUE-owned; per-field zeroize on Drop of consumed sub-seeds is implemented via `ZeroizingSeed` (DC-CRYPTO-08).

_tier: derived · status: enforced · strengthened: PHASE4-N-P_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md §1 (NC-KES-2); docs/planning/phase4-n-p-invariants.md §1 (I6); Cardano Sum6KES specification |
| **Requirement** | KES evolution discipline: evolve(k_i) -> k_{i+1} is one-way. The evolved key signs period i+1 and MUST NOT sign for period i. RED kes_sign is forbidden when the requested period > current_period + evolutions_remaining; kes_evolve is forbidden when to < from or to > from + evolutions_remaining. Forward secrecy is a RED-shell discipline; BLUE has no recovery path if RED violates it. After PHASE4-N-P S5 the underlying algorithm (`ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::update_kes`) is BLUE-owned; per-field zeroize on Drop of consumed sub-seeds is implemented via `ZeroizingSeed` (DC-CRYPTO-08). |

### `DC-CRYPTO-06`: Ade-native KES envelope is the sole accepted hot-signing-key envelope format. Closed grammar `ade.kes.seed.v1`: load-bearing fields {`format`, `role`, `crypto`, `seed_32`, `period_idx`, `format_version`} are validated with `#[serde(deny_unknown_fields)]`; optional metadata {`genesis_hash`, `network_magic`, `created_at_slot`, `created_by`} is ignored but does not break load. The loader returns closed `AdeKesEnvelopeError` variants for every unsupported shape (UnknownEnvelopeFormat, WrongKeyRole, UnsupportedCryptoTag, MissingSeed32, MalformedSeed32, MalformedPeriodIdx, PeriodIdxOutOfRange, UnsupportedFormatVersion, MalformedJson). No fallback parser. No heuristic guess. Private-key bytes never appear in any error/log surface.

_tier: derived · status: enforced_

|--------|----------|

| **Requirement** | Ade-native KES envelope is the sole accepted hot-signing-key envelope format. Closed grammar `ade.kes.seed.v1`: load-bearing fields {`format`, `role`, `crypto`, `seed_32`, `period_idx`, `format_version`} are validated with `#[serde(deny_unknown_fields)]`; optional metadata {`genesis_hash`, `network_magic`, `created_at_slot`, `created_by`} is ignored but does not break load. The loader returns closed `AdeKesEnvelopeError` variants for every unsupported shape (UnknownEnvelopeFormat, WrongKeyRole, UnsupportedCryptoTag, MissingSeed32, MalformedSeed32, MalformedPeriodIdx, PeriodIdxOutOfRange, UnsupportedFormatVersion, MalformedJson). ### `DC-CRYPTO-07`: cardano-cli's `KesSigningKey_ed25519_kes_2^6` envelope (the upstream `Sum6KES` expanded-tree serialization, 608 bytes for a fresh key) is loadable via the Ade-owned BLUE deserializer (`ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes`). After PHASE4-N-P S5, structurally-valid 608-byte payloads round-trip into a `KesSecret`; any other payload shape — wrong size (32, 612, anything ≠ 608), malformed sub-tree, inconsistent vk hash, leaf-all-zero, period > 63 tree shape — fail-closes via `KeyLoadError::UnsupportedExpandedKesKeyFormat` (size mismatch) or `KeyLoadError::KesParse(KesParseError::*)` (structural defect). No fallback parser; the deserializer IS the structural validator.

_tier: derived · status: enforced · strengthened: PHASE4-N-P_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-O/S1.md §1; docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/S5.md; docs/active/op-ops-04-ade-native-kes-flow.md |
| **Requirement** | cardano-cli's `KesSigningKey_ed25519_kes_2^6` envelope (the upstream `Sum6KES` expanded-tree serialization, 608 bytes for a fresh key) is loadable via the Ade-owned BLUE deserializer (`ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes`). After PHASE4-N-P S5, structurally-valid 608-byte payloads round-trip into a `KesSecret`; any other payload shape — wrong size (32, 612, anything ≠ 608), malformed sub-tree, inconsistent vk hash, leaf-all-zero, period > 63 tree shape — fail-closes via `KeyLoadError::UnsupportedExpandedKesKeyFormat` (size mismatch) or `KeyLoadError::KesParse(KesParseError::*)` (structural defect). No fallback parser; the deserializer IS the structural validator. |
| **Code** | crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/keys.rs (load_kes_signing_key_skey routes 608-byte payloads through ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes; wrong-size payloads return UnsupportedExpandedKesKeyFormat) |

### `DC-CRYPTO-08`: Ade-owned Sum6KES algorithm is Haskell-equivalent. `ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes` is byte-identical to Haskell `cardano-base`'s `Sum6KES Ed25519DSIGN`: `derive_verification_key`, `gen_key_kes_from_seed_bytes`, `update_kes` (chain across all 64 periods), and `sign_kes` produce the same bytes as the Haskell reference for every (seed, period, msg) triple. Cross-impl validation against the cardano-cli ground-truth corpus is mechanically enforced under `#[cfg(test)]` only (3 throwaway 608-byte SKEY + VKEY pairs captured from `cardano-cli 11.0.0.0`; deserializing the SKEY through our impl produces the captured VK byte-for-byte). Note: `cardano-crypto` Rust 1.0.8 uses different `expand_seed` prefix bytes (0x00/0x01 vs Haskell's 0x01/0x02) — Ade matches Haskell, NOT cardano-crypto Rust; this divergence is asserted explicitly in `sum6_kes_seed_expansion_diverges_from_cardano_crypto_rust_1_0_8`. After PHASE4-N-P S5, `KesSecret.inner` is the Ade-owned signing key; `cardano-crypto` is a `#[cfg(test)]` oracle only. No compatibility shim may construct an upstream `SumSigningKey` through unsafe layout assumptions, transmute, vendored pub(crate) access, or fork-only constructors (N9), enforced by `ci/ci_check_kes_sum_compatibility.sh` Guard 3.

_tier: derived · status: enforced_

|--------|----------|

| **Requirement** | Ade-owned Sum6KES algorithm is Haskell-equivalent. `ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes` is byte-identical to Haskell `cardano-base`'s `Sum6KES Ed25519DSIGN`: `derive_verification_key`, `gen_key_kes_from_seed_bytes`, `update_kes` (chain across all 64 periods), and `sign_kes` produce the same bytes as the Haskell reference for every (seed, period, msg) triple. Cross-impl validation against the cardano-cli ground-truth corpus is mechanically enforced under `#[cfg(test)]` only (3 throwaway 608-byte SKEY + VKEY pairs captured from `cardano-cli 11.0.0.0`; deserializing the SKEY through our impl produces the captured VK byte-for-byte). Note: `cardano-crypto` Rust 1.0.8 uses different `expand_seed` prefix bytes (0x00/0x01 vs Haskell's 0x01/0x02) — Ade matches Haskell, NOT cardano-crypto Rust; this divergence is asserted explicitly in `sum6_kes_seed_expansion_diverges_from_cardano_crypto_rust_1_0_8`. ### `DC-CRYPTO-09`: Sum6KES expanded signing-key serde and period inference. `raw_serialize_signing_key_kes` / `raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes` are byte-identical to Haskell's `rawSerialiseSignKeyKES` / `rawDeserialiseSignKeyKES` for `Sum6KES Ed25519DSIGN`. The on-disk format is exactly 608 bytes; any other payload size fails closed via `KesParseError::WrongPayloadSize`. `current_period` is uniquely inferable from which sub-seeds are zeroed in the tree (no heuristic; exactly one valid period or a closed parse error) — implemented per the proof obligation at `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/period-from-zeroed-sum6-tree-shape-proof.md`. Round-trip preserves period; serialize → deserialize → serialize yields byte-identical output for every period 0..=63. Malformed sub-trees (truncated child skey, wrong VK length at any recursion level, inconsistent vk0/vk1 hashes, leaf-all-zero) → closed `KesParseError` variant; no best-effort guesswork.

_tier: derived · status: enforced_

|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/cluster.md; docs/planning/phase4-n-p-invariants.md §1 (I3, I5); §2 (N2, N3, N4, N5); docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/period-from-zeroed-sum6-tree-shape-proof.md |
| **Requirement** | Sum6KES expanded signing-key serde and period inference. `raw_serialize_signing_key_kes` / `raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes` are byte-identical to Haskell's `rawSerialiseSignKeyKES` / `rawDeserialiseSignKeyKES` for `Sum6KES Ed25519DSIGN`. The on-disk format is exactly 608 bytes; any other payload size fails closed via `KesParseError::WrongPayloadSize`. `current_period` is uniquely inferable from which sub-seeds are zeroed in the tree (no heuristic; exactly one valid period or a closed parse error) — implemented per the proof obligation at `docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-P/period-from-zeroed-sum6-tree-shape-proof.md`. Round-trip preserves period; serialize → deserialize → serialize yields byte-identical output for every period 0..=63. Malformed sub-trees (truncated child skey, wrong VK length at any recursion level, inconsistent vk0/vk1 hashes, leaf-all-zero) → closed `KesParseError` variant; no best-effort guesswork. |
| **Code** | crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/period.rs (period_from_zeroed_sum6_tree_shape); crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/sum.rs (raw_serialize/raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes); crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/single.rs (Sum0 leaf serde); crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/errors.rs (KesParseError closed surface) |

### `DC-DIFF-01`: Differential harness must localize first divergence point between Ade and reference oracle

_tier: derived · status: partial_

### `DC-LEDGER-08`: Conway cert-state accumulation is a closed, total, era-versioned transition: for each block at track_utxo, certificates decode through the era-correct closed grammar (Conway via the completed single decode_conway_certs retaining all owner payloads, tags 0..18) selected by explicit era dispatch — never the Shelley 6-variant decoder on Conway bytes, never reduced into the 7-variant Shelley Certificate, never with payload fields dropped. Every certificate resolves to an owner-tagged disposition: it mutates B4-owned CertState (delegation/pool), or it is owner-tagged to ConwayGovState and routed out-of-mutation-scope (observed, not swallowed, not applied), or it is a structured reject (NotValidInEra for removed tags 5/6, Malformed for bad CBOR, UnsupportedUntilStateOwner only for genuinely-ownerless cases — unreachable on the real corpus). Composite certs (tags 10/12/13) carry both a B4-owned mutation and an owner-tagged governance effect; both are represented. No certificate is flattened to neutral because there is nowhere to put it (the owner exists), decode-dropped, or apply-swallowed; a decode or apply error propagates as a structured LedgerError and halts the block transition. Incomplete or best-effort accumulation is a forbidden fail-open. (Wiring the owner-tagged ConwayGovState effects into applied governance state is PHASE4-B5, not B4.)

_tier: derived · status: enforced · strengthened: PHASE4-B4_

### `DC-LEDGER-09`: Conway governance-certificate accumulation is a closed, total, era-versioned transition into ConwayGovState: every governance-affecting Conway cert that B4 owner-tagged to ConwayGovState (vote-delegation tags 9/10/12/13 -> vote_delegations; committee tags 14/15 -> committee_hot_keys; DRep tags 16/17/18 -> drep_expiry) resolves to exactly one explicit ConwayGovState mutation or a structured reject -- never observed-and-dropped, never flattened, never with payload fields lost. B5 mutates only governance-owned fields; it does not touch B4-owned CertState and does not double-apply the delegation/pool half of composite certs (10/12/13). DRep expiry is computed only from an explicit gov-env (current epoch + drepActivity); a missing required env input is a structured fail-fast, never a defaulted expiry. A cert that cannot be applied propagates a structured LedgerError and halts the block transition; incomplete or best-effort accumulation is a forbidden fail-open. ConwayGovState becomes a deterministic function of (boundary-loaded base then replayed block-stream cert effects) rather than a frozen snapshot -- a deliberate, oracle-confirmable fingerprint migration (T-DET-01).

### `DC-LEDGER-10`: Credential identity is faithful end-to-end: a stake/committee/DRep credential is a closed sum over {KeyHash, ScriptHash} of a 28-byte hash, never a tag-erased Hash28. Both era certificate decoders preserve the key/script discriminant (an unknown tag is a deterministic reject); the credential type makes a discriminant-less credential unrepresentable on the BLUE authority path (no Hash28->credential coercion); CertState (registrations/delegations/rewards) and ConwayGovState (vote_delegations/committee_hot_keys/drep_expiry) key on the discriminated credential, so a key-hash and a script-hash credential sharing 28 bytes are distinct authoritative-state keys (matching cardano-node's Credential-keyed UMap/VState); and the canonical fingerprint serializes the discriminant so two states differing only in a credential's key/script tag fingerprint differently. The discriminated representation is a deliberate cert-state + gov-state fingerprint migration (T-DET-01). Default scope is Shelley+; Byron is included only if proven to have an affected credential surface.

_tier: derived · status: enforced · strengthened: COMMITTEE-CRED-FIDELITY, DREP-VOTE-FIDELITY, ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-FIDELITY, ENACTMENT-COMMITTEE-WRITEBACK_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Credential = key|script across UTXOW/DELEG/GOVCERT; CIP-1694); IDD illegal-states-unrepresentable + determinism doctrine |
| **Requirement** | Credential identity is faithful end-to-end: a stake/committee/DRep credential is a closed sum over {KeyHash, ScriptHash} of a 28-byte hash, never a tag-erased Hash28. Both era certificate decoders preserve the key/script discriminant (an unknown tag is a deterministic reject); the credential type makes a discriminant-less credential unrepresentable on the BLUE authority path (no Hash28->credential coercion); CertState (registrations/delegations/rewards) and ConwayGovState (vote_delegations/committee_hot_keys/drep_expiry) key on the discriminated credential, so a key-hash and a script-hash credential sharing 28 bytes are distinct authoritative-state keys (matching cardano-node's Credential-keyed UMap/VState); and the canonical fingerprint serializes the discriminant so two states differing only in a credential's key/script tag fingerprint differently. The discriminated representation is a deliberate cert-state + gov-state fingerprint migration (T-DET-01). Default scope is Shelley+; Byron is included only if proven to have an affected credential surface. |

### `DC-PROD-02`: Coordinator slot-tick + forge-result stream replay-equivalence. Wall-clock real-time timestamps and socket arrival order are non-load-bearing RED metadata. Replay is over canonical event streams — NOT real wall-clock time. The forge-result event stream is the canonical surface across the RED-key-custody boundary; the GREEN coordinator is replayable against it without ever seeing secret material.

### `DC-PROD-03`: Producer chain-forward continuity + replay. The GREEN ChainEvolution linear typestate threads each forge's post-state (post-ledger, post-chain_dep, new tip) into the next forge's base; forging against a stale base is structurally unrepresentable (advance consumes self). advance obtains the post-state from BLUE block_validity and the AcceptedBlock token from BLUE self_accept against identical inputs (same pre-forge base, forged bytes, era_schedule, ledger_view); if the two authorities disagree it returns ChainEvolutionError::AuthorityMismatch and does not advance. ChainEvolution never constructs AcceptedBlock directly. For a fixed (bootstrap seed, canonical slot-sequence, KES/VRF/cold keys) the chain-evolution series (block_number, prev_hash, post-ledger fingerprint, post-chain_dep) and the forged block bytes are byte-identical across runs (in-memory two-run; no on-disk replay corpus — durability deferred to N-U).

_tier: derived · status: enforced · strengthened: PHASE4-N-W_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-t-invariants.md §3, §4 (R1, R3); docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-T/cluster.md §1.5, §7 |
| **Requirement** | Producer chain-forward continuity + replay. The GREEN ChainEvolution linear typestate threads each forge's post-state (post-ledger, post-chain_dep, new tip) into the next forge's base; forging against a stale base is structurally unrepresentable (advance consumes self). advance obtains the post-state from BLUE block_validity and the AcceptedBlock token from BLUE self_accept against identical inputs (same pre-forge base, forged bytes, era_schedule, ledger_view); if the two authorities disagree it returns ChainEvolutionError::AuthorityMismatch and does not advance. ChainEvolution never constructs AcceptedBlock directly. For a fixed (bootstrap seed, canonical slot-sequence, KES/VRF/cold keys) the chain-evolution series (block_number, prev_hash, post-ledger fingerprint, post-chain_dep) and the forged block bytes are byte-identical across runs (in-memory two-run; no on-disk replay corpus — durability deferred to N-U). |

### `DC-PROTO-06`: BLUE mini-protocol transitions are pure functions of (canonical prior state, canonical input message, selected protocol version, deterministic configuration); no ambient session-glue state may alter authoritative behavior. Selected version is an explicit input, never read from RED context.

_tier: derived · status: declared · strengthened: PHASE4-N-A, PHASE4-N-G, PHASE4-N-H_

| **Code** | crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/served_chain_handle.rs (push_atomic uses send_modify with served_chain_admit — the established broadcast_to_served drain-and-admit determinism carries through); crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/broadcast_to_served.rs (existing determinism tests cover the underlying invariant; push_atomic is a thin closure around the same primitive) |

### `DC-TXV-06`: For each era, the certificate-deposit classification map(state, cert) is a closed, total, era-versioned function: every certificate variant resolves to exactly one of new_deposit(coin) | refund(coin) | neutral | explicit_reject, with the coin sourced from the cert (Conway explicit-deposit variants, tags 7/8) or the protocol parameter (legacy variants, tags 0/1). An unrecognized cert tag, malformed cert CBOR, or undecodable withdrawals field is a deterministic reject, never a silent neutral. State-dependent cases that cannot be accounted (e.g. pool re-registration charged as a new deposit) reject with a structured UnsupportedStateDependentDepositAccounting error rather than guessing. Incomplete classification is a forbidden false-accept path feeding the value-conservation equation.

_tier: derived · status: enforced · strengthened: PHASE4-B3, PHASE4-B3F_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Cardano ledger spec (Conway CDDL certificate tags 0..18; UTXO deposit/refund accounting); IDD fail-fast + closed-surface doctrine |

An unrecognized cert tag, malformed cert CBOR, or undecodable withdrawals field is a deterministic reject, never a silent neutral. State-dependent cases that cannot be accounted (e.g. pool re-registration charged as a new deposit) reject with a structured UnsupportedStateDependentDepositAccounting error rather than guessing. Incomplete classification is a forbidden false-accept path feeding the value-conservation equation. |
| **Code** | crates/ade_codec/src/conway/cert.rs (decode_conway_certs, closed ConwayCert grammar); crates/ade_codec/src/error.rs (CodecError::UnknownCertTag); crates/ade_types/src/conway/cert.rs (ConwayCert, CertDisposition, DepositEffect, CoinSource); crates/ade_ledger/src/cert_classify.rs (classify); crates/ade_ledger/src/error.rs (UnsupportedStateDependentDepositAccounting); corpus/conway_certs/{classification_table.md,tags.json} |

### `DC-VAL-06`: Every crypto-input, field-size, and structural check on the authority path rejects (produces Invalid) on wrong size or shape and never silently skips. The pattern `if X.len() == K { check } else { skip }` is forbidden in BLUE validation; size checks go through a helper that returns an error. No defined-but-unwired check and no tautological (value-compared-to-itself) guard may stand in for a real check.

_tier: derived · status: enforced · strengthened: PHASE4-B1, PHASE4-B2, PHASE4-B3, PHASE4-B3F_

No defined-but-unwired check and no tautological (value-compared-to-itself) guard may stand in for a real check. |
| **Code** | crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/verdict.rs (FieldKind/FieldError closed fail-closed field taxonomy; PHASE4-B1-S3); crates/ade_core/src/consensus/kes_check.rs (expect_size fail-closed header crypto-field guard; PHASE4-B1-S5); crates/ade_testkit/src/validity/adversarial.rs (M1 truncated VRF proof, M3 flipped KES sig, M4 slot-beyond-horizon adversarial mutators exercising the fail-closed checks; PHASE4-B1-S7); crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/witness.rs (wrong-size vkey/sig → MalformedWitnessField via from_bytes, never skipped); crates/ade_ledger/src/tx_validity/required_signers.rs (unresolvable input / malformed certs|withdrawals|voters CBOR → structured RequiredSignerError, never silent skip; PHASE4-B2-S1); crates/ade_ledger/src/conway.rs (check_conway_coin_conservation: closed coin-level preservation-of-value check wired into validate_conway_state_backed — closes the state-backed fail-open gap where outputs+fee != inputs was accepted at track_utxo=true; PHASE4-B2-S4); crates/ade_testkit/src/tx_validity/adversarial.rs (GREEN witness/value/input mutators driving tx_validity fail-closed; PHASE4-B2-S4) |

### `CN-CINPUT-01`: SeedEpochConsensusInputs closed type + SOLE version-gated byte-canonical codec

_tier: constraint · status: enforced · introduced: PHASE4-N-F-A_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-A/cluster.md; A1-seed-epoch-consensus-inputs-type.md |
| **Requirement** | The seed-epoch consensus inputs (epoch, active-slots coefficient, total active stake, per-pool active-stake + registered VRF keyhash distribution) persisted as Ade recovered state MUST be a single closed canonical type (`SeedEpochConsensusInputs`) with a SOLE encoder/decoder pair: deterministic CBOR, BTreeMap-ordered (no HashMap), version-gated (decode rejects any version `!= SEED_CINPUT_SCHEMA_VERSION` fail-closed), and byte-canonical (a structurally valid but non-canonically-encoded buffer is rejected, never silently re-canonicalized). No second encoder/decoder for this type may exist. |
| **Code** | crates/ade_ledger/src/seed_consensus_inputs.rs (`SeedEpochConsensusInputs` + `encode_`/`decode_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs` + `SeedConsensusInputsError`) |
| **Tests** | `seed_epoch_consensus_inputs_round_trips_byte_identical`, `seed_cinput_decode_rejects_unknown_version`, `seed_cinput_decode_rejects_noncanonical_or_duplicate_keys` |
| **CI** | _(no CI script — gap)_ |

### `CN-CINPUT-02`: Bootstrap-only sidecar population + forge-time containment fence

_tier: constraint · status: enforced · introduced: PHASE4-N-F-A_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-A/cluster.md; A2-bootstrap-population-containment.md; A3a-wal-provenance-entry.md |
| **Requirement** | The `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` sidecar MUST be populated ONLY on the verified-bootstrap composition path (`genesis_bootstrap` / `mithril_bootstrap`), through the anchor-fp-keyed `SnapshotStore` surface (`put_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs`), built via the GREEN merge (`merge_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs`) and the A1 sole encoder. The forge-time consensus-inputs path (`produce_mode` / `import_live_consensus_inputs` / `pool_distr_view_from_consensus_inputs` / `--consensus-inputs-path`) MUST NOT build or put the sidecar, nor append its WAL provenance. Enforced by a data-flow-resistant containment gate (global call-site scan, not a bypassable RHS grep). **This rule constrains POPULATION + the forge-time fence only**; it does NOT assert that the producer CONSUMES the recovered surface — producer consumption is deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C and no registry rule is introduced for it in this close. |
| **Code** | crates/ade_runtime/src/genesis_bootstrap.rs; crates/ade_runtime/src/mithril_bootstrap.rs; crates/ade_runtime/src/seed_consensus_merge.rs; crates/ade_runtime/src/seed_consensus_provenance.rs; ci/ci_check_consensus_input_provenance.sh |
| **Tests** | `bootstrap_persists_anchor_keyed_seed_consensus_inputs`, `bootstrap_seed_inputs_merge_fails_closed_on_missing_vrf_or_stake`, `snapshot_store_keyed_sidecar_is_disjoint_from_slot_snapshots` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_consensus_input_provenance.sh` — fails the build if any production (test-stripped) site outside `{genesis_bootstrap.rs, mithril_bootstrap.rs, seed_consensus_provenance.rs}` calls `.put_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs(` / `merge_seed_epoch_consensus_inputs(` / `append_seed_epoch_provenance(`, or if `produce_mode.rs` names any sidecar build/put/encode token. |

> **Open obligation (deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C, NOT a defect).** Populate-side + forge-time-fence enforced. The CONSUME-side fence (the gate must also reject `RequiredFromRecoveredProvenance` / `seed_epoch_consensus_source` tokens in `produce_mode`) and producer consumption of the recovered surface (**CE-A-4b**) are deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C; no registry rule is introduced for that consumption path until N-F-C scopes/promotes it. Until then `produce_mode` passes only `SeedEpochConsensusSource::NotRequired` and cannot name the recovered type. (BA-02 is NOT claimed satisfied; `produce_mode` still uses `--consensus-inputs-path`.)

### `CN-CONS-07`: Self-acceptance bridge: a forged block is NOT eligible for RED broadcast unless Ade's own header validator (PHASE4-N-B path) and body validator (PHASE4-B1 path) accept it under the same slot, era, and context. Self-acceptance failure halts the producer deterministically. RED broadcast is gated on the BLUE self-accept verdict.

_tier: release · status: enforced · strengthened: PHASE4-N-G, PHASE4-N-H_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md §1 (NC-SELF-1) |
| **Requirement** | Self-acceptance bridge: a forged block is NOT eligible for RED broadcast unless Ade's own header validator (PHASE4-N-B path) and body validator (PHASE4-B1 path) accept it under the same slot, era, and context. Self-acceptance failure halts the producer deterministically. RED broadcast is gated on the BLUE self-accept verdict. |
| **Code** | crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/self_accept.rs (self_accept, AcceptedBlock, SelfAcceptError); crates/ade_ledger/src/block_validity/transition.rs (block_validity — single closed validator authority self_accept wraps); crates/ade_ledger/src/producer/served_chain.rs (ServedChainSnapshot, served_chain_admit — only AcceptedBlock values may enter the served-chain index; PHASE4-N-G S2 strengthening preserves the broadcast gate across the network seam); crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/admitted.rs (AdmittedBlock, admit_via_block_validity — PHASE4-N-H mirror: receive-side admission gate via the same block_validity authority; symmetric to AcceptedBlock); crates/ade_ledger/src/receive/chain_write.rs (ChainDbWrite trait takes AdmittedBlock by value) |

### `CN-FORGE-01`: The producer-mode forge handler is a closed transition from CoordinatorEvent::RequestForge { slot, kes_period, ledger_snapshot_ref, chain_tip } to exactly one of three ForgeResult variants: ForgeSucceeded { slot, artifact } where artifact.bytes decodes via Ade's BLUE block decoder AND self_accept(artifact, chain_tip, ledger_snapshot) returns Accepted; ForgeNotLeader { slot, vrf_output_fingerprint }; or ForgeFailed { slot, structured_error }. No other outcome is permitted. ForgeSucceeded MUST NOT be emitted if self_accept rejects the artifact — the handler emits ForgeFailed { SelfAcceptRejected } instead. Empty-block forging is the explicit scope; mempool integration is out of scope for the rule's enforcement evidence.

### `CN-FORGE-02`: Leader-check splits across the RED/BLUE color boundary: RED produces a VRF proof/output for the slot using the operator's VRF signing key; BLUE verifies the proof and evaluates leader eligibility from canonical inputs only (slot, eta0, stake_distribution, leader_threshold, vrf_vk, vrf_proof_or_output, LeaderScheduleAnswer). BLUE never sees the VRF / KES / cold signing keys. The BLUE evaluator (`verify_and_evaluate_leader`) lives at `ade_core::consensus::leader_check` and has no dependency on LedgerView, EraSchedule, ChainDepState, wall-clock, storage, or RED crates. Caller derives LeaderScheduleAnswer via the authority path (query_leader_schedule) and passes it in. The closed two-variant LeaderCheckVerdict (Eligible carries forge-capable material; NotEligible carries only bounded vrf_output_fingerprint evidence) makes illegal observation of forge-capable material structurally impossible.

### `CN-FORGE-03`: Producer/validator codec symmetry: forge_block emits the era-tagged [era, block] envelope (era = Conway discriminant 7) via the single canonical ade_codec::encode_block_envelope (symmetric to decode_block_envelope), so forge_block output round-trips through the SAME decode_block authority that validates received blocks. decode_block(forge_block(tick).bytes) is Ok and yields a DecodedBlock whose header-body fields and four preserved body-bucket bytes equal what was forged. A bare-block (no-envelope) forge output, or any forge<->decode asymmetry, is CI-gated impossible. Root cause (PHASE4-N-T): forge_block emitted a bare array(5) block, so decode_block_envelope rejected EVERY forged block at offset 0 (BlockValidityError::Body(Decoding(InvalidStructure))) before any header/KES/leader/self_accept logic.

### `CN-FORGE-04`: Producer-side Praos VRF construction must match the Conway/Praos validator authority: the leader VRF proof alpha, the leader-schedule evidence, the LeaderScheduleAnswer.expected_vrf_input contract, and the self_accept header verification must all use ONE era-correct Praos construction. For Conway/Praos the producer alpha MUST equal the validator alpha (praos_vrf_input(slot, eta0) = blake2b256(slot||eta0) + vrfLeaderValue range-extension), NOT the TPraos role-tagged alpha (slot||eta0||0x4C). No verification/construction fallback may accept both TPraos and Praos VRF inputs — for a given era/protocol version there is exactly one VRF transcript authority.

### `CN-GENESIS-01`: The Shelley genesis closed-contract parser accepts a real cardano-cli `shelley-genesis.json` and produces a canonical `GenesisAnchor`. Required fields (networkMagic, systemStart, slotLength, slotsPerKESPeriod, maxKESEvolutions) fail-closed on missing / malformed / wrong-type input. No implicit defaults (e.g., 'if missing, assume preprod' rejected). No stringly fallback (e.g., `"1"` rejected for u32 fields). Extra unknown keys accepted-and-ignored for forward compatibility, iff they do not alter interpretation — the `GenesisAnchor` produced from an extra-key fixture MUST byte-equal the canonical fixture's `GenesisAnchor`. The kes_anchor_slot is operator-supplied (not in genesis) and passed to the parser as a separate argument. systemStart parsing uses a deterministic ISO 8601 → Unix epoch milliseconds conversion (Howard Hinnant proleptic Gregorian).

### `CN-OPCERT-01`: The opcert envelope parser accepts a real cardano-cli `node.opcert` text envelope (closed type check `NodeOperationalCertificate` + CBOR array(2) shape locked by N-R-A A1 OQ4 fixtures against cardano-cli 11.0.0.0 / cardano-node 11.0.1). Element 0 is an array(4) of [hot_vkey(bytes(32)), sequence_number(uint), kes_period(uint), sigma(bytes(64))] mapping to the canonical `OperationalCert`. Element 1 is bytes(32) cold_vk. Any shape mismatch (wrong type field, malformed cborHex, wrong outer/inner arity, wrong field types or lengths) fail-closes with a structured `OpCertParseError` variant. No `String` payloads in load-bearing error variants.

No cross-peer byte leakage is structurally possible — bytes destined for PeerId(a) reach the MuxPump task owning PeerId(a)'s TCP socket, never another peer's.

### `CN-PROD-02`: Producer slot loop never signs a block whose KES period has rotated past current_period. Slot → KES period is a pure function of (slot, genesis_kes_anchor, slots_per_kes_period); the coordinator fail-closes (slot_missed event + log) when wall-clock has advanced past the target slot before forge completes. No retroactive forge. The GREEN coordinator never owns or stores private signing material — it emits a closed `RequestForge { slot, kes_period, ledger_snapshot_ref, chain_tip }` effect; the RED producer shell either returns an `AcceptedBlock` via a `ForgeSucceeded` event or a structured `ForgeFailed { slot, structured_error }` event. KesSecret / VrfSigningKey / ColdSigningKey never enter CoordinatorState. T-tier key-custody boundary.

_tier: derived · status: enforced · strengthened: PHASE4-N-R-A, PHASE4-N-R-C, PHASE4-N-T_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-q-invariants.md §1 (I3, I4, I7, I8); §2 (N4, N5, N8, N9); §5 |
| **Requirement** | Producer slot loop never signs a block whose KES period has rotated past current_period. Slot → KES period is a pure function of (slot, genesis_kes_anchor, slots_per_kes_period); the coordinator fail-closes (slot_missed event + log) when wall-clock has advanced past the target slot before forge completes. No retroactive forge. The GREEN coordinator never owns or stores private signing material — it emits a closed `RequestForge { slot, kes_period, ledger_snapshot_ref, chain_tip }` effect; the RED producer shell either returns an `AcceptedBlock` via a `ForgeSucceeded` event or a structured `ForgeFailed { slot, structured_error }` event. KesSecret / VrfSigningKey / ColdSigningKey never enter CoordinatorState. T-tier key-custody boundary. |

### `CN-WIRE-08`: N2N tag-24 CBOR-in-CBOR payload envelopes are constructed and stripped through ONE shared BLUE byte authority in ade_codec (wrap_tag24/unwrap_tag24). Protocol-specific composition lives in ade_network BLUE codecs: a served BlockFetch MsgBlock payload is tag24(bytes([era,block])) (era inside the wrap); a served ChainSync RollForward header is [era_tag, tag24(bytes(header_cbor))] (era_tag outside the wrap). Both compositions are pinned byte-identically against captured cardano-node 11.0.1 wire fixtures, not codec comments. No bare [era,block] may be served over BlockFetch and no bare header over ChainSync RollForward. No hand-rolled tag-24 parse may exist in RED — admission and interop call the shared authority. unwrap_tag24 fails closed (typed error) on non-(0xd8 0x18), wrong inner length, or trailing bytes. The inner bytes are copied verbatim (no re-encode).

_tier: derived · status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-x-invariants.md |
| **Requirement** | N2N tag-24 CBOR-in-CBOR payload envelopes are constructed and stripped through ONE shared BLUE byte authority in ade_codec (wrap_tag24/unwrap_tag24). Protocol-specific composition lives in ade_network BLUE codecs: a served BlockFetch MsgBlock payload is tag24(bytes([era,block])) (era inside the wrap); a served ChainSync RollForward header is [era_tag, tag24(bytes(header_cbor))] (era_tag outside the wrap). Both compositions are pinned byte-identically against captured cardano-node 11.0.1 wire fixtures, not codec comments. No bare [era,block] may be served over BlockFetch and no bare header over ChainSync RollForward. No hand-rolled tag-24 parse may exist in RED — admission and interop call the shared authority. unwrap_tag24 fails closed (typed error) on non-(0xd8 0x18), wrong inner length, or trailing bytes. | **Code** | crates/ade_codec/src/cbor/tag24.rs (wrap_tag24/unwrap_tag24 + TagEnvelopeError); crates/ade_codec/src/cbor/mod.rs (read_bytes/read_text/skip_item length-arg overflow guard — fail-closed, no panic); crates/ade_network/src/codec/block_fetch.rs + chain_sync.rs (per-protocol compose/decompose); crates/ade_network/src/block_fetch/server.rs + chain_sync/server.rs (serve emits composed bytes); crates/ade_node/src/admission/runner.rs + crates/ade_core_interop/src/follow.rs (RED unwraps migrated onto the shared authority) |
| **Tests** | `wrap_then_unwrap_is_identity_across_length_classes`, `wrap_emits_canonical_tag24_marker_and_length`, `unwrap_returns_zero_copy_borrow_of_input`, `unwrap_rejects_missing_tag24_marker`, `unwrap_rejects_non_byte_string_payload`, `unwrap_rejects_truncated_inner`, `unwrap_rejects_trailing_bytes`, `inner_bytes_are_verbatim_not_reencoded`, `unwrap_rejects_huge_declared_length_without_panic`, `read_bytes_rejects_overflowing_declared_length`, `read_text_rejects_overflowing_declared_length`, `producer_block_fetch_serve_block_payload_is_tag24_wrapped_and_decodes`, `producer_block_fetch_serve_block_bytes_equal_accepted_block_as_bytes`, `block_body_is_wrapped_cbor_item`, `captured_block_era_index_matches_ade_storage_scheme`, `chain_sync_wire_era_index_is_consensus_index`, `compose_decompose_rollforward_header_round_trips`, `decompose_rollforward_header_rejects_non_tag24_inner`, `conway_rollforward_header_served_shape_matches_oracle`, `producer_chain_sync_serve_roll_forward_header_equals_accepted_block_header_bytes`, `session_transcript_served_block_bytes_equal_admitted_accepted_block_bytes`, `session_transcript_announced_header_matches_served_body_recipe`, `cross_impl_server_pipeline_request_range_returns_decodable_bytes`, `cross_impl_server_pipeline_request_range_byte_identical_to_self_accept_input` |

## RO — Release Obligations

Release obligations — properties that must hold before the project ships a release (live-pass evidence, genesis/Mithril import, sync-evidence manifests, close-gate discipline, test-corpus presence).

_15 rules._

### `RO-CLOSE-01`: Unmasked close-gate discipline. Any slice that changes canonical bytes, encoded forms, decoder inputs, or golden fixtures MUST run an UNMASKED full close gate (cargo test --workspace) and use cargo's REAL exit status / result line as the sole pass/fail authority for cluster closure. Piped output (| tail, | grep) may be used for display only, NEVER as the pass/fail authority — a pipeline's exit code is the last stage's, not cargo's. Before closure, ALL consumers of the changed canonical output (every golden fixture, decoder, re-encode, and byte-identity test, across all crates — not just the edited crate) MUST be grepped/audited. A cluster is not closed until the unmasked close gate exits successfully.

_tier: release · status: enforced_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-V/CLOSURE.md; user-direction (PHASE4-N-V close correction) |
| **Requirement** | Unmasked close-gate discipline. Any slice that changes canonical bytes, encoded forms, decoder inputs, or golden fixtures MUST run an UNMASKED full close gate (cargo test --workspace) and use cargo's REAL exit status / result line as the sole pass/fail authority for cluster closure. Piped output (| tail, | grep) may be used for display only, NEVER as the pass/fail authority — a pipeline's exit code is the last stage's, not cargo's. Before closure, ALL consumers of the changed canonical output (every golden fixture, decoder, re-encode, and byte-identity test, across all crates — not just the edited crate) MUST be grepped/audited. A cluster is not closed until the unmasked close gate exits successfully. |
| **Code** | process/release discipline — no BLUE code locus; binds /cluster-close and any slice touching canonical output |
| **Tests** | _(no tests named in registry — gap)_ |
| **CI** | _(no CI script — gap)_ |

### `OP-OPS-04`: Operator-supplied keys. Ade supports both KES key flows: (a) Ade-native `ade_node --mode key_gen_kes --out-file PATH` emitting an `ade.kes.seed.v1` envelope loaded via `ade_runtime::producer::keys::load_ade_kes_signing_key`; (b) cardano-cli `node key-gen-KES` emitting a 608-byte `KesSigningKey_ed25519_kes_2^6` envelope loaded via `ade_runtime::producer::keys::load_kes_signing_key_skey`. After PHASE4-N-P S5 the cardano-cli path routes through the Ade-owned BLUE deserializer (`ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes`); both flows produce a `KesSecret` whose inner is `ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::SigningKey` (BLUE-owned algorithm). VRF and cold (Ed25519) keys continue to be operator-supplied via cardano-cli text-envelope `.skey` files. Private-key material never crosses into BLUE — the entire RED custody surface lives under `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/{keys,signing,ade_kes_envelope}.rs`. Wrong-size payloads fail-close via `KeyLoadError::UnsupportedExpandedKesKeyFormat`; structurally-invalid 608-byte payloads fail-close via `KeyLoadError::KesParse(KesParseError::*)`. Mechanical enforcement: ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh + ci/ci_check_kes_envelope_closed.sh + ci/ci_check_kes_sum_compatibility.sh.

_tier: operational · status: enforced · strengthened: PHASE4-N-O, PHASE4-N-P_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md §7 (OQ1); docs/active/op-ops-04-ade-native-kes-flow.md; docs/planning/phase4-n-p-invariants.md |
| **Requirement** | Operator-supplied keys. After PHASE4-N-P S5 the cardano-cli path routes through the Ade-owned BLUE deserializer (`ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes`); both flows produce a `KesSecret` whose inner is `ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::SigningKey` (BLUE-owned algorithm). Every crate named in a **Code** row is present in CODEMAP: `ade_codec`, `ade_core`, `ade_core_interop`, `ade_crypto`, `ade_ledger`, `ade_network`, `ade_node`, `ade_plutus`, `ade_runtime`, `ade_testkit`, `ade_types`. No crate-level mismatch. - **CI count delta:** CODEMAP stamps **103** `ci_check_*.sh` gates at `3b78008`; at HEAD `67d1ccc` there are **105** — the +2 since the CODEMAP baseline are `ci_check_registry_code_locus_exists.sh` (added by `5db9aae`, the registry-integrity meta-gate) and `ci_check_mithril_seed_point_independence.sh` (added by PHASE4-N-Z, the seed-point-independence containment gate, bound to DC-MITHRIL-02 / CN-MITHRIL-01 / RO-MITHRIL-IMPORT-01). CODEMAP's CI count is therefore two behind HEAD. Reconcile on the next CODEMAP regeneration; no rule is mis-traced (the meta-gate is intentionally unbound to a single rule — see below).

The last is a deliberate **registry-integrity meta-gate**, not a per-rule gate: it validates that every `crates/**.rs` and `ci/**.sh` path named in any registry `code_locus` exists on disk (it guards the registry itself, so it cannot be attributed to a single invariant). It is correctly absent from any rule's **CI** row by design. **101 of 105** on-disk `ci_check_*.sh` gates are rule-bound; the 4 unbound are these (3 hygiene + 1 meta-gate).

## Honest enforcement gaps (standing)

The four-cell contract is filled for every `enforced` rule (Code + Tests + CI all present and verified on disk at HEAD `67d1ccc` via grep/ls — no build/test was run this pass). The standing gaps below are recorded rather than hidden.

- **`declared` rules (113) are open enforcement gaps by design.** Each carries `_(no enforcing code located — gap)_` / `_(no tests named in registry — gap)_` / `_(no CI script — gap)_` cells. These are named-but-not-yet-mechanically-enforced invariants; the gap is the actionable backlog, not a defect to paper over.

- **RO-MITHRIL-IMPORT-01 — `partial` (provenance + production-wiring; seed-bytes + fixture still open).** PHASE4-N-Z **closed item (b)**: `bootstrap_from_mithril_snapshot` is now the wired production composition (verify-before-bootstrap, fail-closed via the closed `MithrilBootstrapError`), and the data-flow-resistant containment gate `ci_check_mithril_seed_point_independence.sh` structurally CI-blocks re-tautologization — the bound anchor's `seed_point` must originate from the operator's independent seed-point inputs, **never** the Mithril manifest (this neutralises the re-tautologization hazard flagged in the S7 security re-review: if the two compared origins ever collapse to one, the binding would compare a value to itself and become vacuous). The new enforced rule DC-MITHRIL-02 carries this contract; CN-MITHRIL-01 is `strengthened_in += PHASE4-N-Z`. **Status stays `partial`** — two items remain: (a) seed-*bytes*-from-Mithril decode (option B) — needs a Mithril artifact-type spike + forward-replay; (c) a committed reproducible Mithril fixture + CI/release evidence. `blocked_until_mithril_seed_bytes_and_fixture`.

- **DC-CINPUT-01 — `partial` (warm-start verification capability proven; PRODUCTION restart path deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C).** The warm-start seed-epoch-consensus-input restore is proven on the AUTHORITY SURFACE (A3b): `bootstrap_initial_state(RequiredFromRecoveredProvenance)` restores the sidecar byte-identically and fail-closed (hash, anchor_fp, epoch_no, re-encode byte-identity), backed by the 12 `wal_seed_cinput_*` / `replay_*` / `warm_start_*` tests, all of which resolve on disk at HEAD `a3a0636`. The **PRODUCTION restart path** — a production mode that opens a persistent store + `FileWalStore`, replays to a `RecoveredBootstrapProvenance`, and threads `bootstrap_initial_state` — is NOT wired (`node.rs` `run_node_until_shutdown` + `recover_node_state` are test-only; `produce_mode` cold-starts). This is a **deferred obligation (PHASE4-N-F-C, C3), not a defect**: the capability is enforced; only the production wiring is owed. `blocked_until_production_recovery_mode_threads_warm_start`. **No CI gate** binds DC-CINPUT-01 (its enforcement is the test suite); this is a standing CI gap for the rule.

- **CE-A-4b (producer consumption of the recovered surface) — deliberately NOT promoted this close.** The producer does not yet CONSUME the projected recovered `PoolDistrView` / eta0 on the bounty-primary forge path; `produce_mode` still uses `--consensus-inputs-path` and passes only `SeedEpochConsensusSource::NotRequired`. CN-CINPUT-02 (population + forge-time fence) and DC-CINPUT-02a (projection equivalence) bound everything PHASE4-N-F-A ships; producer consumption is tracked solely in the CN-CINPUT-02 / DC-CINPUT-01 `open_obligation` fields and is **deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C**. **No DC-CINPUT-02b / producer-consumption registry rule is introduced** — by design, until N-F-C scopes and promotes it. BA-02 is therefore NOT claimed satisfied by this close.

- **RO-SYNC-EVIDENCE-01 — `partial` (vacuous-until-committed).** The schema + sha256 gate (`ci_check_sync_evidence_manifest_schema.sh`) is enforced but **vacuously satisfied** until an operator commits a manifest (it mirrors the CN-OPERATOR-EVIDENCE-01 pattern). The two-Haskell-node private-Conway-testnet snapshot→tip live capture is **operator-witnessed**: `blocked_until_operator_pass_executed` (CE-Y-16). It flips to enforcing content the moment a CE-Y-16 manifest lands.

- **CE-Y-16 (operator-witnessed live leg).** The snapshot→tip differential sync against two real Haskell nodes is the live evidence backing DC-COMPAT-01 and RO-SYNC-EVIDENCE-01. DC-COMPAT-01 is `enforced` for the *mechanism* (the differential harness + the forbidden-fingerprint-equality gate run in CI), but the *witnessed live capture* is an operator pass not yet executed — the same class as the CN-CONS-06 / RO-LIVE-01 operator-pass leg tracked under the operator-pass C1 follow-on.

- **Governance note — CE-not-law (mechanism vs. authority).** Several PHASE4-N-Y/N-Z enforcement points are **cluster-mechanical-acceptance (CE) gates**, not constitutional-law (true-tier) enforcement, and the distinction is load-bearing:
  - `bootstrap_initial_state` is enforced as the *single* genesis→initial-state authority by `ci_check_mithril_uses_bootstrap_initial_state.sh` (a text/structure gate) plus `genesis_path_fp_equals_snapshot_path_fp` (an Ade-vs-Ade fingerprint-equality test). This proves the two Ade construction paths agree; it does **not** prove agreement with cardano-node serialized state — and DC-COMPAT-01 explicitly **forbids** asserting Ade-fingerprint == Haskell-state-hash.
  - The Mithril seed-point-independence guarantee (DC-MITHRIL-02) is enforced by a closed `MithrilBootstrapError` fail-close at the single composition site plus the data-flow `ci_check_mithril_seed_point_independence.sh` containment gate (a grep-class structural gate against laundering the manifest's point-bearing fields into the anchor `seed_point`), backed by three targeted tests. Breadth across future composition sites is the CI text-gate's responsibility, not a type-level impossibility.
  - The forward-sync durability ordering (DC-SYNC-01: bytes + WAL durable *before* AdvanceTip) is structurally enforced by a private `AdmitPlan` with a single `durable()` emit site and a RED `TipBeforeDurable` fail-close, backed by the **two-driver** replay test (`forward_sync_replay_two_runs_byte_identical`) and the chokepoint gate. Breadth across all future call sites is a CI text-gate (`ci_check_forward_sync_chokepoint_only.sh`), a grep — not a type-level impossibility.
  - The `WalEntry` recovery-reconciliation invariant (DC-SYNC-01 S6: a torn `put_block`/wal-append crash cannot incorporate an un-WAL'd orphan) is proven by a single targeted crash-injection test (`recovery_torn_put_block_before_wal_append_drops_orphan`) over the modelled torn-write point — a CE-level guarantee at that injection point, not an exhaustive proof across all crash interleavings.

  None of these are regressions — they are the honest boundary between *mechanism enforced now* and *authority claimed*, recorded so the next cluster can decide whether to promote any from CE-gate to true-tier law.

---

## Generation notes

Regenerated from the registry (`docs/ade-invariant-registry.toml`, 303 rules) as primary source; tests and CI scripts cross-checked against the working tree at HEAD `a3a0636` using **grep/ls only** — no `cargo build`/`cargo test`/`cargo check` was run. Test existence is verified against the leaf function name (segment after the last `::`) over all `fn` definitions under `crates/**.rs`; CI existence is verified by basename against `ci/ci_check_*.sh`. Both the `ci_script` (comma-joined string) and `ci_scripts` (array) registry fields are read for the **CI** row. The registry is parsed with a TOML parser, so multi-line array and triple-quoted-string fields are read correctly (the prior pass fixed a multi-line-array parsing bug; this pass keeps that — every `tests = [` array, single- or multi-line, resolves).

HEAD `a3a0636` is the **PHASE4-N-F-A close** (seed-epoch consensus-input provenance — anchor-bound *recovered* surface; capability cluster, not production wiring). Delta vs the `67d1ccc` (PHASE4-N-Z) pass: **+4 rules** (now 303):

- **CN-CINPUT-01** (`enforced`, `constraint`) — `SeedEpochConsensusInputs` closed type + SOLE version-gated byte-canonical codec. Code `crates/ade_ledger/src/seed_consensus_inputs.rs`; 3 tests; **no CI gate** (the type's codec discipline is test-enforced).
- **CN-CINPUT-02** (`enforced`, `constraint`) — bootstrap-only sidecar population + forge-time containment fence. Code across `genesis_bootstrap.rs` / `mithril_bootstrap.rs` / `seed_consensus_merge.rs` / `seed_consensus_provenance.rs`; 3 tests; CI `ci/ci_check_consensus_input_provenance.sh` (data-flow-resistant global call-site containment, verified executable + exits non-zero on FAIL at HEAD `a3a0636`).
- **DC-CINPUT-01** (`partial`, `derived`) — warm-start verification CAPABILITY at the authority surface. Code `wal/event.rs` / `wal/replay.rs` / `seed_consensus_provenance.rs` / `bootstrap.rs`; 12 tests (all resolve on disk); **no CI gate**. Its `open_obligation` is the PRODUCTION restart path, deferred to PHASE4-N-F-C — `partial`, not a defect (see Honest enforcement gaps).
- **DC-CINPUT-02a** (`enforced`, `derived`) — projection equivalence (recovered surface → `PoolDistrView` + eta0). Code `consensus_view.rs` + reused `vrf_cert.rs::leader_vrf_input`; 4 tests; **no CI gate**.
